Program support is provided on musescore.org.\r\n\r\n\r\nFeatures supported by MuseScore include:\r\n\r\n* Unlimited score length\r\n* Unlimited number of staves per system\r\n* Up to four independent voices per staff\r\n* Score creation wizard and templates\r\n* Guitar, bass, ukulele, lute tablature\r\n* Automatic part extraction and transposition\r\n* Repeats, including segnos, codas, and measure repeats\r\n* Dynamics, articulations, and other expression markings, with playback support for most\r\n* Custom text markings\r\n* Lyrics\r\n* Chord symbols\r\n* Jazz notation, including lead sheets, slash notation and a “handwritten” font for text\r\n* Swing and shuffle playback\r\n* Mixer for instrument levels and effects\r\n* Percussion notation\r\n* Early music notation\r\n* Cross-staff beaming\r\n* Import of graphics\r\n* Custom key signatures\r\n* Additive time signatures\r\n* User-defined score styles\r\n\r\nMost elements in MuseScore are laid out automatically but can also be positioned manually. is a free and open-source vector graphics editor; it can be used to create or edit vector graphics such as illustrations, diagrams, line arts, charts, logos and complex paintings. Inkscape's primary vector graphics format is Scalable Vector Graphics (SVG), however many other formats can be imported and exported.\r\n\r\nInkscape can render primitive vector shapes (e.g. rectangles, ellipses, polygons, arcs, spirals, stars and 3D boxes) and text. These objects may be filled with solid colors, patterns, radial or linear color gradients and their borders may be stroked, both with adjustable transparency.
